&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;How to Configure SAP Connection on Informatica Cloud After the Summer 2016 Release&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;This troubleshooting wizard is an interactive flowchart to help you isolate and resolve your issues. The questions asked and steps provided here are intended to help you solve the issue through self-service.&lt;/p&gt;<div>&lt;p&gt;Choose the situation that is closest to what you are experiencing, and we will take you through the problem-solving process step-by-step.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After the Summer 2016 release of Informatica Cloud, the SAP Connector will no longer be using the Classic SAP RFC SDK's. This change has been incorporated since these SDKs has been brought to End Of Life by SAP.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The SAP Connector now uses the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK 7.20 libraries for the following tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Processing data through RFCs/BAPIs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reading IDocs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Writing IDocs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Writing data to SAP tables&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This guide will help you in configuring the SAP Type connection for&amp;nbsp;the above mentioned connectivity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the Operating System&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#da0be610-3a01-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backda0be610-3a01-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Linux&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#b6432a60-3a18-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Contact SAP Technical Support&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Contact SAP Customer Support if you encounter issues while downloading the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK libraries.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back3b08cc70-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3b08cc70-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3b08cc70-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;317fb5c0-3a1b-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Configuring JCO Libraries and Secure Agent&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP&amp;nbsp;JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the SAP JCO libraries from the SAP marketplace. Ensure that the libraries downloaded are of the correct bit mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 60px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;\main\bin\rdtm-extra\tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the &lt;em&gt;tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt; directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl\sap directory does not exist.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;3. Configure the JAVA_LIBS property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Type&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;list, select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for the Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: Windows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: ../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar;../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK &lt;/em&gt;to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did the Secure Agent restart successfully?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#bdf06710-3a12-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e764bab0-3a03-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backbdf06710-3a12-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#e764bab0-3a03-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note&lt;/em&gt;: &lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you have created the 300620 and 447900 plugin folders earlier, delete the &lt;em&gt;sapjco3.jar &lt;/em&gt;file from both the plugin folders after you upgrade the SAP Connector. &lt;br /&gt;The 300620 and 447900 folders contains the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file. You must retain the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file in both the plugin folders.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; to access the &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click &lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the &lt;em&gt;Type&lt;/em&gt; list, select &lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Linux&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: &lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-&amp;nbsp;extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar:../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c27bbb90-3a12-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e764bab0-3a03-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc27bbb90-3a12-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#e764bab0-3a03-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note&lt;/em&gt;: &lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you have created the 300620 and 447900 plugin folders earlier, delete the &lt;em&gt;sapjco3.jar &lt;/em&gt;file from both the plugin folders after you upgrade the SAP Connector. &lt;br /&gt;The 300620 and 447900 folders contains the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file. You must retain the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file in both the plugin folders.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; to access the &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click &lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the &lt;em&gt;Type&lt;/em&gt; list, select &lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Linux&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: &lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-&amp;nbsp;extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar:../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;\main\bin\rdtm-extra\tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note&lt;/em&gt;:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you have created the 300620 and 447900 plugin folders earlier, delete the &lt;em&gt;sapjco3.jar&lt;/em&gt; file from both the plugin folders after you upgrade the SAP Connector. &lt;br /&gt;The 300620 and 447900 folders contains the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file. You must retain the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file in both the plugin folders.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; property in Informatica Cloud:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for Windows secure agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Windows&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value:&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar;../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back45681650-39fc-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#45681650-39fc-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#45681650-39fc-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c046d930-3a1d-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Configuring SAPNWRFC.INI&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Creating the sapnwrfc.ini File&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named sapnwrfc.ini. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the sapnwrfc.ini file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the sapnwrfc.ini file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameter&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Applicable Connection Types&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;DEST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#47168e00-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#47168e00-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP&amp;nbsp;JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the SAP JCO libraries from the SAP marketplace. Ensure that the libraries downloaded are of the correct bit mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 60px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;\main\bin\rdtm-extra\tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the &lt;em&gt;tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt; directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl\sap directory does not exist.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;3. Configure the JAVA_LIBS property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Type&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;list, select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for the Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: Windows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: ../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar;../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK &lt;/em&gt;to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#4ffe9070-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#47168e00-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back4ffe9070-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#47168e00-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP&amp;nbsp;JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the SAP JCO libraries from the SAP marketplace. Ensure that the libraries downloaded are of the correct bit mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 60px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;\main\bin\rdtm-extra\tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the &lt;em&gt;tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt; directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl\sap directory does not exist.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;3. Configure the JAVA_LIBS property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Type&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;list, select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for the Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: Windows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: ../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar;../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK &lt;/em&gt;to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note&lt;/em&gt;: &lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you have created the 300620 and 447900 plugin folders earlier, delete the &lt;em&gt;sapjco3.jar &lt;/em&gt;file from both the plugin folders after you upgrade the SAP Connector. &lt;br /&gt;The 300620 and 447900 folders contains the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file. You must retain the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file in both the plugin folders.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; to access the &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt; page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click &lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the &lt;em&gt;Type&lt;/em&gt; list, select &lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for Linux Secure Agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Linux&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value: &lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-&amp;nbsp;extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar:../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;\main\bin\rdtm-extra\tpl\sap&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note&lt;/em&gt;:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;Before coping the JCo files, create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you have created the 300620 and 447900 plugin folders earlier, delete the &lt;em&gt;sapjco3.jar&lt;/em&gt; file from both the plugin folders after you upgrade the SAP Connector. &lt;br /&gt;The 300620 and 447900 folders contains the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file. You must retain the &lt;em&gt;tpl.properties&lt;/em&gt; file in both the plugin folders.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; property in Informatica Cloud:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Type&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;list, select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the &lt;em&gt;JAVA_LIBS&lt;/em&gt; value for Windows secure agent as follows:&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Windows&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value:&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar;../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#471204b0-3a1b-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#41925a90-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back471204b0-3a1b-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#41925a90-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back8fceeaa0-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#8fceeaa0-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#8fceeaa0-3a17-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;3b5960a0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#8cd969a0-3a1d-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3b5960a0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back8cd969a0-3a1d-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#3b5960a0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Creating the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; File &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt;. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;: If you have an existing saprfc.ini, remove and create a sapnwrfc.ini file based on the following parameters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameter &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Applicable Connection Types &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;DEST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system  for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be  unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and  later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight  characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;Run the tasks that uses the SAP Connector.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#931c3220-3a1d-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3b5960a0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back931c3220-3a1d-11e6-9fec-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#3b5960a0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Creating the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; File &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt;. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;: If you have an existing saprfc.ini, remove and create a sapnwrfc.ini file based on the following parameters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Creating the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; File &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt;. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;: If you have an existing saprfc.ini, remove and create a sapnwrfc.ini file based on the following parameters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameter &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Applicable Connection Types &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;DEST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system  for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be  unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and  later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight  characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Use this parameter for the  following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&#159; Connection  to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;197&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP   gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;ASHOST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host  name or IP address of the SAP application. The Secure Agent uses this entry  to attach to the application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to a specific SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to a specific SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Group  name of the SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;PROGRAM_ID&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Program  ID. The Program ID must be the same as the Program ID for the logical system  that you define in the SAP system to send or receive IDocs.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an  SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host  name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an  SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an  SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;TRACE&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Debugs  RFC connection-related problems.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Set one  of the following values based on the level of detail that you want in the  trace:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;0. Off&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;1. Brief&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;2.  Verbose&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;3. Full&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;3. Full&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#3cae37b0-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c7290840-3a18-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back3cae37b0-3a1a-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#c7290840-3a18-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Download and install the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK 7.20 libraries for Windows Operating System that hosts the Secure Agent. Confirm the Secure Agent bit mode and download the relevant SAP libraries.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To download and install the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK Version 7.20 libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to the &lt;a href=&quot;http://service.sap.com&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;SAP Service Marketplace&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;: You must have SAP credentials to access the Service Marketplace.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download Unicode SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK 7.20 libraries that are specific to Windows Operating System that hosts the Secure Agent.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The following table lists the libraries corresponding to the Windows operating systems (32 and 64 bit):&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#0d1727b0-3a1e-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back0d1727b0-3a1e-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Creating the sapnwrfc.ini File&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named sapnwrfc.ini. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the sapnwrfc.ini file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the sapnwrfc.ini file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameter&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Applicable Connection Types&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;DEST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Use this parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;197&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;ASHOST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host name or IP address of the SAP application. The Secure Agent uses this entry to attach to the application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to a specific SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SYSNR&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP system number.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to a specific SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;R3NAME&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Name of the SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MSHOST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host name of the SAP message server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GROUP&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Group name of the SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;PROGRAM_ID&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Program ID. The Program ID must be the same as the Program ID for the logical system that you define in the SAP system to send or receive IDocs.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GWHOST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GWSERV&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Server name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;TRACE&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Debugs RFC connection-related problems.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Set one of the following values based on the level of detail that you want in the trace:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;0. Off&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;1. Brief&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;2. Verbose&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;3. Full&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Run the tasks that uses the SAP Connector.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#1224a480-3a1e-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back1224a480-3a1e-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#435a05c0-3a1b-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Creating the sapnwrfc.ini File&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named sapnwrfc.ini. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the sapnwrfc.ini file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the sapnwrfc.ini file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt;. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;: If you have an existing saprfc.ini, remove and create a sapnwrfc.ini file based on the following parameters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the &lt;em&gt;sapnwrfc.ini&lt;/em&gt; file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an  SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GWSERV&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Server  name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an  SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;TRACE&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Debugs  RFC connection-related problems.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Set one  of the following values based on the level of detail that you want in the  trace:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;0. Off&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;1. Brief&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;2.  Verbose&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;3. Full&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this  parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;3. Copy the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK libraries to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;4. Set the following permissions for each SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK library:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;nbsp;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Read, write, and execute permissions for the current user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;nbsp;Read and execute permissions for all other users&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backfe3eb6c0-3a01-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#fe3eb6c0-3a01-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#f4e1d6a0-39f9-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#fe3eb6c0-3a01-11e6-a683-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;2874d3f0-3a18-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#0d1727b0-3a1e-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#2874d3f0-3a18-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back0d1727b0-3a1e-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#2874d3f0-3a18-11e6-9079-bc764e10d166');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Creating the sapnwrfc.ini File&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;SAP stores RFC-specific parameters and connection information in a file named sapnwrfc.ini. To enable the Secure Agent to connect to the SAP system as an RFC client, create and configure the sapnwrfc.ini file on the machines that host the Secure Agent.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Create the sapnwrfc.ini file based on the format defined in the following sections and copy the file to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use a DOS editor or WordPad to configure the sapnwrfc.ini file. Notepad can introduce errors to the sapnwrfc.ini file.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameters:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;sapnwrfc.ini Parameter&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Applicable Connection Types&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;DEST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Logical name of the SAP system for the connection.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;All DEST entries must be unique. You must have only one DEST entry for each SAP system.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;For SAP versions 4.6C and later, use up to 32 characters. For earlier versions, use up to eight characters.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;Use this parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;Default&quot;&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Group name of the SAP application server.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to use SAP load balancing.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;PROGRAM_ID&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Program ID. The Program ID must be the same as the Program ID for the logical system that you define in the SAP system to send or receive IDocs.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GWHOST&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Host name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;GWSERV&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Server name of the SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter to create a connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;TRACE&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Debugs RFC connection-related problems.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Set one of the following values based on the level of detail that you want in the trace:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;0. Off&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;1. Brief&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;2. Verbose&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;3. Full&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use this parameter for the following types of connections:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to a specific SAP application server&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to use load balancing&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&#159; Connection to an RFC server program registered at an SAP gateway&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Configure JCO Libraries and Secure Agent&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To configure the SAP JCo libraries, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the SAP JCO libraries from the SAP marketplace. Ensure that the libraries downloaded are of the correct bit mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the JCo libraries to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;:&amp;nbsp;Before you copy the JCo files, you must create the tpl/sap directory within the rdtm-extra directory if the tpl/sap directory does not already exist.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the JAVA_LIBS property in Informatica Cloud.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Cloud.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Configure&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Runtime Environments&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;page.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;To the left of the agent name, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Edit Secure Agent&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;From the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Type&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;list, select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Tomcat JRE&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the JAVA_LIBS value for Linux Secure Agent as follows:&amp;nbsp;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Operating System: &lt;em&gt;Linux&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Value:&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;../bin/rdtm-extra/tpl/sap/sapjco3.jar:../bin/rdtm/javalib/sap/sap-adapter-common.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt; to save the changes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the Secure Agent and run the mapping which uses the SAP connector.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;3 .Copy the SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK libraries to the following directory: &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&amp;lt;Informatica Secure Agent installation directory&amp;gt;/main/bin/rdtm&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Remove the old Classic RFC SDK's from the above location if they still exist.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;4. Set the following permissions for each SAP NetWeaver RFC SDK library: &amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Read, write, and execute permissions for the current user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
